17data_inp 0.001:
SELECT
	t.*,
	COUNT(1) OVER() AS visible_rows
FROM
(
	SELECT
		ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY id DESC) AS rn,
		id,
		current_state,
		filesize,
		report_content,
   		TO_CHAR(d_req, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_req,
   		TO_CHAR(d_last, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_last,
   		id_report,
   		canceled,
   		s_name
	FROM
		t_report_req
	WHERE
		is_enabled = 1 AND
		is_mail = 0 AND
		id_user = :id_user/* AND
		downloaded = 0*/
) t
WHERE
	(:id_req > 0 AND :id_req = t.id) OR
	t.rn BETWEEN :start_num_row AND :last_num_row
bound id_user as INT 21=1 bound start_num_row as INT 21=1 bound last_num_row as INT 21=10 bound id_req as INT 21=0

select a.*, 1-connect_by_isleaf CHILDCOUNT, sys_connect_by_path( id , ',' ) PARENTS , level lvl from(

/*id_organization_merge*/
SELECT
                    id AS id,
                    CASE
                    WHEN regexp_like(sys_context('eaist_context','org'), id||',') THEN null
                    ElSE id_parent
                    END AS parent_id,
                    formatted_name AS name,
                     CASE WHEN (id = '0_2' or id_level=min_level) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS opened, 
                     CASE WHEN (row_count=1 or id_level=min_level or id_level=min_level+1) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS default_selected, 
                    KEY_SORT s_key_sort
                    FROM
                    (select dat.id, dat.id_parent, dat.formatted_name, dat.id_level, f.row_count, dat.KEY_SORT, min(dat.id_level) over() min_level from
                    (
                    select id||'_'||id_source as id, id_parent||'_'||id_parent_source as id_parent, id_level, formatted_name, is_aggregator, rn as KEY_SORT from (
                    SELECT 0 id,2 id_source,NULL id_parent,NULL id_parent_source,1 id_level,'Итого по городу' formatted_name,0 is_aggregator,0 rn FROM DUAL
                    UNION all
                    SELECT
                    	id,id_source,id_parent,id_parent_source,id_level,formatted_name,is_aggregator,rn
                    from sp_customers_tree
                    where version_date=to_date(:version_date,'dd.mm.yyyy') AND is_archive=0                    
                    )) dat
                    
                    join (select f.*, count(*) over() row_count from(
                    select id from lnk_customers_all_level where version_date =to_date(:version_date, 'dd.mm.yyyy') and id_parent in  (select replace(regexp_substr(orgs, '([[:digit:]]*_[[:digit:]]*,)', 1, rownum), ',') org_id
                                                                                                                                      from (select sys_context('eaist_context','org') orgs From dual)
                                                                                                                                      connect by  regexp_count(orgs, '\,')+1>rownum)
                    union
                    select replace(regexp_substr(orgs, '([[:digit:]]*_[[:digit:]]*,)', 1, rownum), ',') org_id
                    from (select sys_context('eaist_context','org') orgs From dual)
                    connect by  regexp_count(orgs, '\,')+1>rownum)f) f on f.id=dat.id
                    WHERE formatted_name NOT IN ('Архив', 'Прочие')
                    
                    )
/**/

) a

start with (parent_id = :START_WITH and :START_WITH is not null) or (:START_WITH is null and parent_id is null) 
 order BY s_key_sort

25granit 0.009:
SELECT
    id,
    parent_id,
    indicator_id,
    name,
    level,
    description,
    DISPLAY_BY_DEFAULT,
    IS_PERIOD,
    IS_BUDGET_YEAR,
    IS_PLAN_PERIOD,
    IS_PLAN_YEAR,
    IS_PERIOD_SEND_REQUEST,
    IS_PERIOD_SEND_CONCLUS,
    ORD,
    IS_FIX_PART
FROM
(
    SELECT
        bh.block_id AS id,
        b.parent_id,
        b.indicator_id,
        b.name,
        i.description_br AS description,
        bh.DISPLAY_BY_DEFAULT,
        b.IS_PERIOD,
        b.IS_BUDGET_YEAR,
        b.IS_PLAN_PERIOD,
        b.IS_PLAN_YEAR,
        b.IS_PERIOD_SEND_REQUEST,
        b.IS_PERIOD_SEND_CONCLUS,
        bh.ORD,
        bh.IS_FIX_PART
    FROM
        s_lnk_block_header bh
    INNER JOIN
        s_sp_block b
        ON
            b.id = bh.block_id
    LEFT JOIN
        f_sp_indicators i
        ON
            i.entity_id = b.indicator_id and :VERSION_DATE between DATE_START and DATE_END 
    WHERE
        bh.header_id IN
        (
            SELECT
                h.id
            FROM
                s_sp_reports r
            INNER JOIN
                s_sp_header h
                ON
                    h.report_id = r.id
            WHERE
                r.id = :REPORT_ID
        )
    ORDER BY
        bh.ORD
)
CONNECT BY
    PRIOR id = parent_id
START WITH
    parent_id IS NULL
    ORDER SIBLINGS BY ORD
bound REPORT_ID as INT 21=19 bound VERSION_DATE as SQLT_CHR good 28.06.2018 (10)

    h.block_id AS id,
    h.header_id,

FROM
    s_lnk_block_header h
LEFT JOIN

    ON
        b.id = h.block_id
WHERE
    h.header_id IN
    (
        SELECT
            h.id
        FROM
            s_sp_reports sp
        LEFT JOIN
            s_sp_header h
            ON
                h.report_id = sp.id
        WHERE
            sp.id = :REPORT_ID
    ) AND
    h.display_by_default = 1
ORDER BY
    h.id
bound REPORT_ID as INT 21=19

/*indicators_tree*/

WITH cols AS
(
    SELECT
        slnk.block_id AS id,
        slnk.header_id,
        b.parent_id,
        b.name
    FROM
        s_lnk_block_header slnk
    LEFT JOIN
        s_sp_block b
        ON
            b.id = slnk.block_id
    WHERE
        slnk.header_id IN
        (
            SELECT
                h.id
            FROM
                s_sp_reports sp
            LEFT JOIN
                s_sp_header h
                ON
                    h.report_id = sp.id
            WHERE
                sp.id = :REPORT_ID
        )
    ORDER BY
        slnk.id
),

cols2 AS
(
    SELECT
        s.id,
        s.name,
        s.parent_id
    FROM
        s_sp_block s
    CONNECT BY
        PRIOR s.parent_id = s.id
    START WITH
        s.id IN (SELECT id FROM cols)
)

SELECT DISTINCT
    id,
    parent_id,
    name,
    1 AS default_selected
FROM
    cols2

17data_inp 0.002:
SELECT
	t.*,
	COUNT(1) OVER() AS visible_rows
FROM
(
	SELECT
		ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY id DESC) AS rn,
		id,
		current_state,
		filesize,
		report_content,
   		TO_CHAR(d_req, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_req,
   		TO_CHAR(d_last, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_last,
   		id_report,
   		canceled,
   		s_name
	FROM
		t_report_req
	WHERE
		is_enabled = 1 AND
		is_mail = 0 AND
		id_user = :id_user/* AND
		downloaded = 0*/
) t
WHERE
	(:id_req > 0 AND :id_req = t.id) OR
	t.rn BETWEEN :start_num_row AND :last_num_row
bound id_user as INT 21=1 bound start_num_row as INT 21=1 bound last_num_row as INT 21=10 bound id_req as INT 21=0

SELECT
	*
FROM
(
	SELECT
		ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY id DESC) AS rn,
		id,
		current_state,
		filesize,
		report_content,
		TO_CHAR(d_req, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_req,
		TO_CHAR(d_last, 'DD.MM.YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS d_last,
		id_report,
		downloaded,
		canceled,
		s_name
	FROM
		T_REPORT_REQ
	WHERE
		is_enabled = 1 AND
		is_mail = 0 AND
		id_user = :id_user
)
WHERE
	rn BETWEEN :start_num_row AND :last_num_row
bound id_user as INT 21=1 bound start_num_row as INT 21=1 bound last_num_row as INT 21=10
